"  -F, --file-name=name          name of generated file  (default=`cmdline')"	*(char)
,	O
"      --output-dir=path         output directory"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  if this option is not specified, the files are generated in the current \n  directory.\n"	*(char)
,	O
"  -c, --c-extension=ext         extension of c file  (default=`c')"	*(char)
,	O
"  -H, --header-extension=ext    extension of header file  (default=`h')"	*(char)
,	O
"  -l, --long-help               long usage line in help"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  The usage line will print all the options, e.g.,\n\n  sample1 -iINT|--int-opt=INT [-h|--help]\n"	*(char)
,	O
"      --default-optional        by default, an option is considered optional if \n                                  not specified otherwise"	*(char)
,	O
"  -u, --unamed-opts[=STRING]    accept options without names (e.g., file names) \n                                   (default=`FILES')"	*(char)
,	O
"\nThe parser generated is thought to be used to parse the command line arguments. \nHowever, you can also generate parsers for configuration files, or strings that \ncontain the arguments to parse, by using the following two options.\n"	*(char)
,	O
"  -C, --conf-parser             generate a config file parser"	*(char)
,	O
"  -S, --string-parser           generate a string parser (the string contains \n                                  the command line)"	*(char)
,	O
"\nAdditional options:"	*(char)
,	O
""	*(char)
,	O
"  -G, --include-getopt          adds the code for getopt_long in the generated \n                                  C file"	*(char)
,	O
"  -n, --no-handle-help          do not handle --help|-h automatically"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  If --no-handle-help is specified, the command line option --help|-h will not \n  be handled automatically, so the programmer will be able to print some other \n  information; then the function for printing the standard help output can be \n  used; this function is called <parser-name>_print_help.\n  \n  Notice that, although the programmer can handle --help|-h manually, the \n  parser will return after finding such option: the other command line options, \n  if any, will be ignored.  In case you want to have full control on --help|-h, \n  you should use --ho-help.\n"	*(char)
,	O
"      --no-help                 do not add --help|-h automatically"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  With this option you can disable the automatic addition of options --help|-h. \n  The programmer will then be able to add this option in the input file and \n  handle it as he sees fit.  Notice that --no-help will also disable the \n  automatic options --detailed-help and --full-help.\n\n  The programmer can still define options with short character h as he wants, \n  but he cannot define options help, unless he specifies --no-help (otherwise \n  an error will be printed).\n"	*(char)
,	O
"  -N, --no-handle-version       do not handle --version|-V automatically"	*(char)
,	O
"      --no-version              do not add --version|-V automatically"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  See above the details about --no-handle-help and --no-help, respectively.\n"	*(char)
,	O
"  -e, --no-handle-error         do not exit on errors"	*(char)
,	O
"  \n  With this option, if the generated parser encounters an error (e.g., an \n  unknown option) it does not make the main program exit; instead, the parser \n  function returns a value different 0, and the main program can print a help \n  message.\n"	*(char)
,	O
"      --show-required[=STRING]  in the output of help will specify which \n                                  options are mandatory, by using the optional \n                                  passed string  (default=`(mandatory)')"	*(char)
,	O
"  -g, --gen-version             put gengetopt version in the generated file  \n                                  (default=on)"	*(char)
,	O
"      --set-package=STRING      set the package name (override package defined \n                                  in the .ggo file)"	*(char)
,	O
"      --set-version=STRING      set the version number (override version \n                                  defined in the .ggo file)"	*(char)
,	O
"      --show-help               show the output of --help instead of generating \n                                  code"	*(char)
,	O
"      --show-full-help          show the output of --full-help (i.e., including \n                                  hidden options) instead of generating code"	*(char)
,	O
"      --show-detailed-help      show the output of --detailed-help (i.e., \n                                  including details and hidden options) instead \n                                  of generating code"	*(char)
,	O
"      --show-version            show the output of --version instead of \n                                  generating code"	*(char)
